### `powershell`

**Poll for Copilot code review**

<details>
<summary>Arguments</summary>

```json
{
  "command": "$REPO = \"edburns/Build26-BRK206-your-agent-anywhere-multiclient-multidevice-with-github-copilot-sdk\"\n$PR = 21\n$TIMEOUT = 600\n$INTERVAL = 30\n$ELAPSED = 0\n\nWrite-Host \"Polling for Copilot review (max 10 min)...\"\n\nwhile ($ELAPSED -lt $TIMEOUT) {\n    $reviews = gh api \"/repos/$REPO/pulls/$PR/reviews\" 2>$null | ConvertFrom-Json\n    $lineComments = gh api \"/repos/$REPO/pulls/$PR/comments\" 2>$null | ConvertFrom-Json\n    \n    # Strategy A\n    $found = $reviews | Where-Object { $_.body -match \"Copilot.s findings\" }\n    # Strategy B\n    if (-not $found) { $found = $reviews | Where-Object { $_.body -match \"Pull request overview\" } }\n    # Strategy C\n    if (-not $found) { $found = $reviews | Where-Object { $_.user.login -match \"copilot-pull-request-reviewer\" } }\n    # Strategy D\n    if (-not $found) { $found = $lineComments | Where-Object { $_.user.login -eq \"Copilot\" } | Select-Object -First 1 }\n    \n    if ($found) {\n        Write-Host \"Copilot review found after $ELAPSED seconds!\"\n        break\n    }\n    \n    Write-Host \"[$ELAPSED s] No review yet, waiting $INTERVAL s...\"\n    Start-Sleep -Seconds $INTERVAL\n    $ELAPSED += $INTERVAL\n}\n\nif ($ELAPSED -ge $TIMEOUT) {\n    Write-Host \"TIMEOUT: Copilot review not posted within 10 minutes\"\n} else {\n    Write-Host \"Review detected!\"\n}\n",
  "description": "Poll for Copilot code review",
```

### `powershell`

**Fetch full Copilot review body and comments**

<details>
<summary>Arguments</summary>

```json
{
  "command": "$REPO = \"edburns/Build26-BRK206-your-agent-anywhere-multiclient-multidevice-with-github-copilot-sdk\"\n$PR = 21\n\n# Get full review body\n$reviews = gh api \"/repos/$REPO/pulls/$PR/reviews\" | ConvertFrom-Json\n$copilotReview = $reviews | Where-Object { $_.user.login -match \"copilot-pull-request-reviewer\" }\nWrite-Host \"=== FULL REVIEW BODY ===\"\nWrite-Host $copilotReview.body\nWrite-Host \"========================\"\n\n# Get line-level comments\n$lineComments = gh api \"/repos/$REPO/pulls/$PR/comments\" | ConvertFrom-Json\n$copilotComments = $lineComments | Where-Object { $_.user.login -match \"copilot-pull-request-reviewer|Copilot\" }\nWrite-Host \"`n=== LINE COMMENTS (Count: $($copilotComments.Count)) ===\"\n$copilotComments | ForEach-Object {\n    Write-Host \"ID: $($_.id)\"\n    Write-Host \"Path: $($_.path)\"\n    Write-Host \"Line: $($_.line)\"\n    Write-Host \"Body: $($_.body)\"\n    Write-Host \"---\"\n}\n",
  "description": "Fetch full Copilot review body and comments"
}
```

</details>

```
=== FULL REVIEW BODY ===
## Pull request overview

Implements the Java demo’s end-to-end “real-time pipeline UI” update chain (Jakarta Faces push → PrimeFaces partial update → post-update CSS transitions) and scaffolds the minimal backend model/state to drive the pipeline in the BRK206 real-estate agent orchestrator.

**Changes:**
- Added PrimeFaces/JSF front-end pieces for live pipeline refresh (`f:websocket` + `p:remoteCommand`) and post-update animations (JS + CSS).
- Introduced backend pipeline scaffolding: phases, UI push bean, application state/agent execution, and JSF view helpers.
- Added Jakarta Data/JPA property model + repository + seed + Copilot tool for property search.

<details>
<summary>Show a summary per file</summary>

| File | Description |
| ---- | ----------- |
| src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/resources/js/pipeline.js | Handles websocket push events, triggers remoteCommand refresh, and applies animation/state classes after DOM patching. |
| src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/resources/css/pipeline.css | Dark-theme pipeline layout and transition/pulse styles for phase changes. |
| src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/index.xhtml | Wires `p:remoteCommand` + `f:websocket` and renders the pipeline grid with `data-*` state for client-side class toggling. |
| src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/UiUpdateSocket.java | CDI wrapper around Faces `PushContext` for broadcasting pipeline updates. |
| src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/PropertyDatabase.java | Seeds sample properties and exposes a `@CopilotTool` property search. |
| src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/Property.java | JPA entity for property listings. |
| src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/PipelineView.java | JSF backing bean providing phase/agent collections and CSS-class helpers. |
| src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/Phase.java | Pipeline phase enum matching the C# demo’s high-level flow. |
| src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/data/PropertyRepository.java | Jakarta Data repository interface for property persistence and queries. |
| src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/AppState.java | Application-scoped orchestrator state: manages agents, runs sessions on virtual threads, schedules rejected-agent removal, owns CopilotClient lifecycle. |
| src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/Agent.java | Agent session implementation and Copilot SDK tool wiring (annotated tools + lambda tool + cross-class tools). |
</details>

## Review details





- **Files reviewed:** 11/11 changed files
- **Comments generated:** 5
- **Review effort level:** Low



========================

=== LINE COMMENTS (Count: 5) ===
ID: 3547991362
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/index.xhtml
Line: 32
Body: `p:commandButton` uses `update="@none"`, but the action adds `FacesMessage`s (and the input has `requiredMessage`). With an Ajax submit, messages won't be re-rendered, so users won't see validation/warn messages. Update at least the messages component.
---
ID: 3547991378
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/data/PropertyRepository.java
Line: 29
Body: The Jakarta Data `@Query` strings use an undeclared alias (`p`). Per this repo's Jakarta Data guidance, range queries should use JDQL field names without an alias (e.g., `WHERE bedrooms >= ?1`), otherwise these methods will fail at runtime when invoked.
---
ID: 3547991394
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/Agent.java
Line: 123
Body: On session failures, the catch block can overwrite a successfully-completed agent (`phase == DONE`) with `REJECTED_GARBAGE`, because it only excludes the two rejection phases. This can produce incorrect UI state and triggers rejected-agent removal scheduling. Only force a rejection when the agent is not already in a terminal phase.
---
ID: 3547991404
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/PropertyDatabase.java
Line: 57
Body: This Javadoc says "Any parameter may be null or empty", but `minBedrooms` and `maxPriceGbp` are primitives and can’t be null/empty. This is misleading for tool consumers and future maintainers; document the actual sentinel behavior (0 = no filter).
---
ID: 3547991421
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/resources/js/pipeline.js
Line: 60
Body: `phase` is read from `data-phase` but never used, which is dead code and can confuse future readers. Remove it (or use it) to keep the refresh logic minimal.
---
```

```
50.  *

54. function onPipelineRefreshed() {
55.     console.log('[Pipeline] DOM updated — applying animation classes.');
56. 
57.     var cards = document.querySelectorAll('.agent-card');
58. 
59.     cards.forEach(function (card) {
60.         var phase = card.getAttribute('data-phase');
61.         var active = card.getAttribute('data-active') === 'true';
62.         var rejected = card.getAttribute('data-rejected') === 'true';
63.         var done = card.getAttribute('data-done') === 'true';
64. 
65.         // Remove existing state classes before reapplying
66.         card.classList.remove('active', 'completed', 'rejected');
67. 
68.         if (rejected) {
69.             card.classList.add('rejected');
70.         } else if (done) {
71.             card.classList.add('completed');
72.         } else if (active) {
73.             card.classList.add('active');
```

### `view`

**view the file at C:\Users\edburns\workareas\review-copilot-pr-21\src\java-agent-orchestrator\src\main\java\com\microsoft\build\realestate\Phase.java.**

C:\Users\edburns\workareas\review-copilot-pr-21\src\java-agent-orchestrator\src\main\java\com\microsoft\build\realestate\Phase.java

<details>
<summary>37 lines</summary>

```
1. package com.microsoft.build.realestate;
2. 
3. /**
4.  * Pipeline phases matching the C# demo's Phase enum.
5.  * Agents move through the main sequence (QUEUED → VALIDATING → SEARCHING → WRITING_REPORT → DONE)
6.  * or branch to a terminal rejection phase.
7.  */
8. public enum Phase {
9.     QUEUED("Queued"),
10.     VALIDATING("Validating"),
11.     SEARCHING("Searching"),
12.     WRITING_REPORT("Writing Report"),
13.     REJECTED_GARBAGE("Rejected"),
14.     REJECTED_NO_MATCHES("No Matches"),
15.     DONE("Done");
16. 
17.     private final String label;
18. 
19.     Phase(String label) {
20.         this.label = label;
21.     }
22. 
23.     public String getLabel() {
24.         return label;
25.     }
26. 
27.     /** Returns true if this phase is a terminal (finished) state. */
28.     public boolean isTerminal() {
29.         return this == DONE || this == REJECTED_GARBAGE || this == REJECTED_NO_MATCHES;
30.     }
31. 
32.     /** Returns true if this phase is a rejection state. */
33.     public boolean isRejected() {
34.         return this == REJECTED_GARBAGE || this == REJECTED_NO_MATCHES;
35.     }
36. }
37.
```

</details>

### `powershell`

```json
{
  "command": "$REPO = \"edburns/Build26-BRK206-your-agent-anywhere-multiclient-multidevice-with-github-copilot-sdk\"\n$PR = 21\n$OWNER = \"edburns\"\n$REPONAME = \"Build26-BRK206-your-agent-anywhere-multiclient-multidevice-with-github-copilot-sdk\"\n\n# Get review threads with their first comment database IDs\n$threads = gh api graphql -F number=$PR -F owner=$OWNER -F repo=$REPONAME -f query='\nquery($number: Int!, $owner: String!, $repo: String!) {\n  repository(owner: $owner, name: $repo) {\n    pullRequest(number: $number) {\n      reviewThreads(first: 100) {\n        nodes {\n          id\n          isResolved\n          comments(first: 1) { nodes { databaseId } }\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}' | ConvertFrom-Json\n\n$threads.data.repository.pullRequest.reviewThreads.nodes | ForEach-Object {\n    Write-Host \"Thread ID: $($_.id), Resolved: $($_.isResolved), First comment DB ID: $($_.comments.nodes[0].databaseId)\"\n}\n",
  "description": "Get review thread IDs for resolution"
}
```

<sub>23m 6s</sub>

### `powershell`

**Poll for 2nd Copilot review iteration**

<details>
<summary>Arguments</summary>

```json
{
  "command": "$REPO = \"edburns/Build26-BRK206-your-agent-anywhere-multiclient-multidevice-with-github-copilot-sdk\"\n$PR = 21\n$TIMEOUT = 600\n$INTERVAL = 30\n$ELAPSED = 0\n$KNOWN_REVIEW_IDS = @(4658676143)  # ID of the first Copilot review - need to track\n\n# First get existing review IDs to detect only new ones\n$existingReviews = gh api \"/repos/$REPO/pulls/$PR/reviews\" | ConvertFrom-Json\n$existingIds = $existingReviews | Where-Object { $_.user.login -match \"copilot-pull-request-reviewer\" } | Select-Object -ExpandProperty id\nWrite-Host \"Existing Copilot review IDs: $existingIds\"\n\nWrite-Host \"Polling for NEW Copilot review (iteration 2, max 10 min)...\"\n\nwhile ($ELAPSED -lt $TIMEOUT) {\n    $reviews = gh api \"/repos/$REPO/pulls/$PR/reviews\" 2>$null | ConvertFrom-Json\n    $lineComments = gh api \"/repos/$REPO/pulls/$PR/comments\" 2>$null | ConvertFrom-Json\n    \n    # Look for a new review from copilot-pull-request-reviewer\n    $newReviews = $reviews | Where-Object { \n        $_.user.login -match \"copilot-pull-request-reviewer\" -and \n        $existingIds -notcontains $_.id \n    }\n    \n    # Also check for new line comments newer than the existing review\n    $newComments = $lineComments | Where-Object { $_.user.login -match \"copilot-pull-request-reviewer|Copilot\" }\n    \n    if ($newReviews) {\n        Write-Host \"New Copilot review found after $ELAPSED seconds! ID: $($newReviews.id)\"\n        Write-Host \"Body preview: $($newReviews.body.Substring(0, [Math]::Min(300, $newReviews.body.Length)))\"\n        break\n    }\n    \n    Write-Host \"[$ELAPSED s] No new review yet, waiting $INTERVAL s...\"\n    Start-Sleep -Seconds $INTERVAL\n    $ELAPSED += $INTERVAL\n}\n\nif ($ELAPSED -ge $TIMEOUT) {\n    Write-Host \"TIMEOUT: No new Copilot review posted within 10 minutes\"\n}\n",
  "description": "Poll for 2nd Copilot review iteration",
  "initial_wait": 120,
  "mode": "sync",
  "shellId": "poll3"
}
```

```
ID: 3548031383
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/index.xhtml
Line: 27
Body: `h:inputText` sets `requiredMessage` but not `required`, so JSF required-field validation will never trigger and the attribute is effectively dead/misleading. Either add `required="true"` (recommended) or drop `requiredMessage` and rely solely on the action-method check.
---
ID: 3548031391
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/index.xhtml
Line: 35
Body: Using `onclick="this.disabled=true"` and `oncomplete="this.disabled=false"` relies on `this` being the button element in the Ajax callback; that context is not reliable and can leave the button stuck disabled. PrimeFaces has built-in support for this via `disableOnAjax="true"`.
---
ID: 3548031402
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/AppState.java
Line: 94
Body: If the removal virtual thread is interrupted (e.g., during shutdown), it currently still removes the agent and pushes an `agent-removed` event. After restoring the interrupt flag, return early so interruption actually cancels the scheduled removal work.
---
ID: 3548031418
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/Agent.java
Line: 127
Body: `CopilotSession.close()` exceptions are currently swallowed, which can hide resource/transport issues and make debugging shutdown leaks difficult. Log the exception at least at WARNING so failures are visible in server logs.
---
ID: 3548031430
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/Agent.java
Line: 138
Body: `String.toUpperCase()` is locale-sensitive; in certain locales this can produce unexpected results and break `Phase.valueOf(...)`. Use `toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT)` (and trim) for deterministic parsing of tool input.
---
ID: 3548031445
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/resources/js/pipeline.js
Line: 82
Body: This comment says only the "currently-active" card pulses, but the selector applies `pulse-indicator` to *every* `.agent-card.active` dot. Update the comment to match the implemented behavior (or change the selector if only one card should pulse).
---
<shellId: 22 completed with exit code 0>
```

```
85.      * Schedules removal of a rejected agent after the linger period.
86.      * After removal, pushes an agent-removed event so the browser clears the card.
87.      */
88.     private void scheduleRemoval(String agentId) {
89.         Thread.ofVirtual().name("removal-" + agentId).start(() -> {
90.             try {
91.                 Thread.sleep(REJECTED_LINGER_MS);
92.             } catch (InterruptedException e) {
93.                 Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
94.             }
95.             agents.remove(agentId);
96.             uiUpdateSocket.pushAgentRemoved(agentId);
97.         });
98.     }
99. 
100.     @PreDestroy
101.     public void shutdown() {
102.         try {
103.             copilotClient.close();
104.         } catch (Exception e) {
105.             LOG.warning("Error closing CopilotClient: " + e.getMessage());
106.         }
107.     }
108. }
```

```
Line: 136
Body: The system prompt and Javadoc refer to the tool name `set_current_phase`, but this method is registered via `@CopilotTool` without an explicit `name`. If the SDK defaults the tool name to the Java method name (`setCurrentPhase`), the model will try to call `set_current_phase` and fail, preventing phase updates and breaking the UI pipeline.
---
ID: 3548060079
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/PropertyDatabase.java
Line: 59
Body: The agent prompt instructs the model to call the `search_properties` tool, but this method is registered via `@CopilotTool` without an explicit `name`. If the SDK uses the Java method name (`searchProperties`) as the tool name, tool calls to `search_properties` will fail at runtime.
---
ID: 3548060089
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/PropertyDatabase.java
Line: 74
Body: `String.toLowerCase()` is locale-sensitive. For deterministic filtering (and to match the locale-safe parsing already used elsewhere in this PR), use `toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)` for both the input and the property field.
---
ID: 3548060096
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/PropertyDatabase.java
Line: 80
Body: Same locale-sensitivity issue here: use `toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)` for deterministic matching.
---
ID: 3548060109
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/PipelineView.java
Line: 48
Body: `AppState` stores agents in a `ConcurrentHashMap`, whose iteration order is unspecified. Rendering the UI from that order can cause cards within a phase to reshuffle between refreshes, making the real-time updates look glitchy. Sort deterministically (e.g., by `startedAt` or id) before returning the list.
---
ID: 3548060122
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/resources/js/pipeline.js
Line: 79
Body: `setTimeout` is scheduled on every refresh without cancelling any previously scheduled removal for the same card. If pushes arrive faster than 400ms, an older timer can remove the `transitioning` class early and cancel the newer transition. Store the timeout id on the element and clear it before scheduling a new one.
---
ID: 3548060139
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/index.xhtml
Line: 122
Body: `f:websocket` can start receiving messages as soon as the page connects, but `pipeline.js` (which defines `handlePipelinePush`) is currently targeted to `body`, meaning the handler may not exist yet if a push arrives during initial page load. Load the script in `head` so the handler functions are defined before the WebSocket can dispatch messages.
---
```

```
89.                 .toList();
90.         }
```

```
54. function onPipelineRefreshed() {
55.     console.log('[Pipeline] DOM updated — applying animation classes.');
56. 
57.     var cards = document.querySelectorAll('.agent-card');
58. 
59.     cards.forEach(function (card) {
60.         var active = card.getAttribute('data-active') === 'true';
61.         var rejected = card.getAttribute('data-rejected') === 'true';
62.         var done = card.getAttribute('data-done') === 'true';
63. 
64.         // Remove existing state classes before reapplying
65.         card.classList.remove('active', 'completed', 'rejected');
66. 
67.         if (rejected) {
68.             card.classList.add('rejected');
69.         } else if (done) {
70.             card.classList.add('completed');
71.         } else if (active) {
72.             card.classList.add('active');
73.         }
74. 
75.         // Apply the transitioning class briefly to produce a visible scale effect
76.         card.classList.add('transitioning');
77.         setTimeout(function () {
78.             card.classList.remove('transitioning');
79.         }, 400);
80.     });
81. 
82.     // Update pulse indicators: all currently-active cards' status dots pulse
83.     var allDots = document.querySelectorAll('.status-dot');
84.     allDots.forEach(function (dot) {
85.         dot.classList.remove('pulse-indicator');
86.     });
87. 
88.     var activeDots = document.querySelectorAll('.agent-card.active .status-dot');
89.     activeDots.forEach(function (dot) {

91.     });
92. }
```

```
1. package com.microsoft.build.realestate;
2. 
3. import com.github.copilot.CopilotClient;
4. import com.github.copilot.CopilotClientMode;
5. import com.github.copilot.CopilotClientOptions;
6. import jakarta.annotation.PreDestroy;
7. import jakarta.enterprise.context.ApplicationScoped;
8. import jakarta.inject.Inject;
9. import java.nio.file.Path;
10. import java.util.Collection;
11. import java.util.Collections;
12. import java.util.Map;
13. import java.util.UUID;
14. import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
15. import java.util.logging.Logger;
16. 
17. /**
18.  * Application-scoped CDI bean that owns the CopilotClient and manages the
19.  * collection of active agent sessions.
20.  *
21.  * <p>Equivalent to the C# {@code AppState} class. All state is concurrent-safe
22.  * because multiple virtual threads may submit new enquiries simultaneously.
23.  */
24. @ApplicationScoped
25. public class AppState {
26. 
27.     private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(AppState.class.getName());
28. 
29.     /** How long (ms) a rejected agent stays visible before being removed. */
30.     private static final long REJECTED_LINGER_MS = 15_000L;
31. 
32.     private final CopilotClient copilotClient;
33.     private final Map<String, Agent> agents = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
34. 
35.     @Inject
36.     private PropertyDatabase propertyDatabase;
37. 
38.     @Inject
39.     private UiUpdateSocket uiUpdateSocket;
40. 
41.     public AppState() {
42.         String copilotHome = Path.of(System.getProperty("user.home"), ".copilot").toString();
43.         this.copilotClient = new CopilotClient(
44.                 new CopilotClientOptions()
45.                         .setMode(CopilotClientMode.EMPTY)
46.                         .setCopilotHome(copilotHome));
47.     }
48. 
49.     /**
50.      * Submits a new enquiry and launches an agent session on a virtual thread.
51.      *
52.      * @param enquiry the customer's natural-language enquiry text
53.      * @return the new agent's ID
54.      */
55.     public String submitEnquiry(String enquiry) {
56.         String agentId = UUID.randomUUID().toString().replace("-", "").substring(0, 8);
57.         Agent agent = new Agent(agentId, enquiry, propertyDatabase, uiUpdateSocket);
58.         agents.put(agentId, agent);
59.         uiUpdateSocket.pushPhaseChange(agentId);
60. 
61.         Thread.ofVirtual().name("agent-" + agentId).start(() -> {
62.             try {
63.                 agent.run(copilotClient);
64.             } finally {
65.                 if (agent.isRejected()) {
66.                     scheduleRemoval(agentId);
67.                 }
68.             }
69.         });
70. 
71.         return agentId;
72.     }
73. 
74.     /** Returns an unmodifiable view of all current agents (active, done, and pending removal). */
75.     public Collection<Agent> getAgents() {
76.         return Collections.unmodifiableCollection(agents.values());
77.     }
78. 
79.     /** Returns the agent with the given ID, or {@code null} if not found. */
80.     public Agent getAgent(String agentId) {
81.         return agents.get(agentId);
82.     }
83. 
84.     /**
85.      * Schedules removal of a rejected agent after the linger period.
```

```
51.         this.enquiry = enquiry;
52.         this.propertyDatabase = propertyDatabase;
53.         this.uiUpdateSocket = uiUpdateSocket;
54.     }
55. 
56.     /**
57.      * Runs the agent session against the given CopilotClient.
58.      * Blocks (on a virtual thread) until the session completes.
59.      */
60.     public void run(CopilotClient client) {
61.         SystemMessageConfig systemMessage = new SystemMessageConfig()
62.                 .setMode(SystemMessageMode.CUSTOMIZE);
63.         systemMessage.getSections().put(SystemMessageSection.IDENTITY,
64.                 new SectionOverride()
65.                         .setAction(SectionOverrideAction.REPLACE)
66.                         .setContent("""
67.                             You are part of a real estate recommendation system. You will receive enquiries
68.                             from customers, and you must carry out the following workflow. As you proceed,
69.                             update your current phase and intent, which will be visible to the user.
70.                             Do not stop until the phase reaches a final state.
71.                             Start by setting phase to "VALIDATING".
72. 
73.                             - Validation phase
74.                               - Check the enquiry is genuine and not spam, garbage, or off-topic.
75.                               - If it's not genuine, set phase to "REJECTED_GARBAGE" and stop.
76.                             - Search phase
77.                               - Extract relevant search criteria and search our property listings.
78.                               - To search our property listings, call the search_properties tool.
79.                                 You may call it multiple times with different filters to refine results.
80.                               - If the customer is looking for a neighbourhood with a particular feature,
81.                                 always perform at least one web search to confirm locations.
82.                               - At the end of this phase, if you don't find any relevant properties,
83.                                 set phase to "REJECTED_NO_MATCHES" and stop.
84.                             - Report phase
85.                               - Write up a report for our salesperson to use when calling the customer.
86.                               - Your report should include a summary of the customer's needs and the top
87.                                 1-3 matching properties. For each property, include key selling points.
88.                               - At the end of this phase, set phase to "DONE" and stop.
89. 
90.                             Always use set_current_phase each time you enter a new phase, and report your
91.                             intent at each step.
92.                             """));
93. 
94.         // report_intent as inline lambda (ToolDefinition.from) — demonstrates ADR-006 style
95.         ToolDefinition reportIntentTool = ToolDefinition
96.                 .from("report_intent",
97.                       "Reports the current intent of the agent",
98.                       Param.of(String.class, "intent", "Intent in max 4 words"),
99.                       (String intent) -> { currentIntent = intent; notifyUi(); return "ok"; })
100.                 .overridesBuiltInTool(true);
101. 
102.         // @CopilotTool annotated methods on this instance — demonstrates ADR-005 style
103.         List<ToolDefinition> annotatedTools = ToolDefinition.fromObject(this);
104. 
105.         // search_properties from PropertyDatabase — demonstrates cross-class @CopilotTool
106.         List<ToolDefinition> dbTools = ToolDefinition.fromObject(propertyDatabase);
107. 
108.         SessionConfig sessionConfig = new SessionConfig()
109.                 .setOnPermissionRequest(PermissionHandler.APPROVE_ALL)
110.                 .setSystemMessage(systemMessage)
111.                 .setAvailableTools(List.of("*"))
112.                 .setTools(concatLists(annotatedTools, dbTools, List.of(reportIntentTool)));
113. 
114.         try {
115.             session = client.createSession(sessionConfig).get();
```

```
Total comments retrieved: 42
Comments in review 4658875333: 6
ID: 3548099832, Login: Copilot
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/index.xhtml
Body: `data-phase` is rendered on each agent card, but nothing in `pipeline.js` (or elsewhere in `src/main/webapp`) reads it. Keeping unused `data-*` attributes makes the DOM harder to reason about and suggests client-side phase logic that no longer exists.
---
ID: 3548099844, Login: Copilot
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/index.xhtml
Body: `pipelineView.getAgentsAtPhase(phase)` is evaluated multiple times per phase column (here and again in the empty-placeholder check). Because agents are updated concurrently, those calls can observe different snapshots in the same render, causing inconsistent markup (e.g., cards rendered plus an empty placeholder). Cache the list in a Facelets variable and reuse it.
---
ID: 3548099854, Login: Copilot
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/index.xhtml
Body: This empty-column check calls `pipelineView.getAgentsAtPhase(phase)` again, which can disagree with the list used to render the cards if agents are added/removed mid-render. Reuse the cached `agentsAtPhase` list (introduced above) to keep the markup consistent within a request.
---
ID: 3548099870, Login: Copilot
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/Agent.java
Body: The system message requires “at least one web search”, but this PR does not define any web-search tool for the session, so the model may attempt an unavailable tool (or get stuck trying). Also, the prompt asks the agent to “report your intent” without explicitly naming the `report_intent` tool, which makes it less likely the UI intent will update via tool calls. Remove the web-search requirement (or gate it on an available tool) and explicitly instruct calling `report_intent`.
---
ID: 3548099886, Login: Copilot
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/Agent.java
Body: `setAvailableTools(List.of("*"))` grants the session access to all available tools (including any built-ins), which is broader than necessary for this demo and can have security/operational implications (unexpected outbound calls, etc.). Prefer not setting `availableTools` here (or restrict it to an explicit allow-list) since the demo already registers the intended tools via `.setTools(...)`.
---
ID: 3548099911, Login: Copilot
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/PropertyDatabase.java
Body: `@Transactional` is unlikely to be applied on an `@PostConstruct` lifecycle callback (interceptors typically run on business-method invocations via the CDI proxy), so the seeding `save(...)` calls may execute without an active transaction and fail at startup. Delegate from the `@PostConstruct` method to a non-lifecycle `@Transactional` method invoked via the injected CDI proxy.
---
<shellId: 54 completed with exit code 0>
```

```
68.                             from customers, and you must carry out the following workflow. As you proceed,
69.                             update your current phase and intent, which will be visible to the user.
70.                             Do not stop until the phase reaches a final state.
71.                             Start by setting phase to "VALIDATING".
72. 
73.                             - Validation phase
74.                               - Check the enquiry is genuine and not spam, garbage, or off-topic.

78.                               - To search our property listings, call the search_properties tool.
79.                                 You may call it multiple times with different filters to refine results.
80.                               - If the customer is looking for a neighbourhood with a particular feature,
81.                                 always perform at least one web search to confirm locations.
82.                               - At the end of this phase, if you don't find any relevant properties,
83.                                 set phase to "REJECTED_NO_MATCHES" and stop.
84.                             - Report phase
85.                               - Write up a report for our salesperson to use when calling the customer.
86.                               - Your report should include a summary of the customer's needs and the top
87.                                 1-3 matching properties. For each property, include key selling points.
88.                               - At the end of this phase, set phase to "DONE" and stop.
89. 
90.                             Always use set_current_phase each time you enter a new phase, and report your
91.                             intent at each step.
92.                             """));
```

```
New comments: 2
ID: 3548121391
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/PropertyDatabase.java, Line: 30
Body: `@Transactional` on `doSeedDatabase()` will not be applied when it’s invoked via `seedDatabase()` (self-invocation inside the same bean), so the seeding `save(...)` calls can still run without an active transaction at startup. Invoke the transactional method through the CDI proxy (e.g., via an injected `Instance<PropertyDatabase>`), or move seeding into a separate bean.
---
ID: 3548121401
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/index.xhtml, Line: 35
Body: `PipelineView.submitEnquiry()` clears `enquiryText`, but the Ajax `p:commandButton` only updates `msgs`, so the input field won’t be re-rendered/cleared in the browser after submit. Either include `enquiryInput` in the update list or stop mutating `enquiryText` if you want the field to remain populated.
---
<shellId: 60 completed with exit code 0>
```

</details>

```
54.      * JSF action method: submits the enquiry text to AppState and launches an agent.
55.      */
56.     public void submitEnquiry() {
57.         if (enquiryText == null || enquiryText.isBlank()) {
58.             FacesContext.getCurrentInstance().addMessage(null,
59.                     new FacesMessage(FacesMessage.SEVERITY_WARN,
60.                             "Please enter an enquiry.", null));
61.             return;
62.         }
63.         String agentId = appState.submitEnquiry(enquiryText.trim());
64.         LOG.info("Submitted enquiry, agent ID: " + agentId);
65.         enquiryText = "";
66.     }
67. 
68.     /**
69.      * Returns the CSS class(es) for a phase column header.
70.      * Used in index.xhtml to avoid complex inline EL ternary expressions.
71.      */
72.     public String getPhaseHeaderClass(Phase phase) {
73.         if (phase == Phase.DONE) {
74.             return "phase-header done";
75.         }
76.         if (phase.isRejected()) {
77.             return "phase-header rejected";
78.         }
79.         return "phase-header";
80.     }
```

```
2.

4. import com.github.copilot.tool.annotation.CopilotToolParam;

6. import jakarta.annotation.PostConstruct;
7. import jakarta.enterprise.context.ApplicationScoped;
8. import jakarta.inject.Inject;
9. import jakarta.transaction.Transactional;
10. import java.util.List;
11. import java.util.Locale;
12. import java.util.logging.Logger;
13. 
14. /**
15.  * CDI bean that manages the real-estate property database.
16.  * Seeds the database with sample listings on startup.
17.  * Exposes a searchProperties tool for the Copilot SDK agents.
18.  */
19. @ApplicationScoped
20. public class PropertyDatabase {
21. 
22.     private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(PropertyDatabase.class.getName());
23. 
24.     @Inject
25.     private PropertyRepository repository;
26. 
27.     @PostConstruct
28.     public void seedDatabase() {
29.         doSeedDatabase();
30.     }
31. 
32.     @Transactional
33.     public void doSeedDatabase() {
34.         long count = repository.findAll().count();
35.         if (count > 0) {
36.             LOG.info("Property database already seeded with " + count + " properties.");
37.             return;
38.         }
39.         LOG.info("Seeding property database...");
40.         repository.save(new Property("Semi-detached house", "London", "Hackney",        3, 750_000, "Victorian terrace, south-facing garden, 5 min walk to Hackney Central station."));
41.         repository.save(new Property("Flat",                "London", "Canary Wharf",   2, 520_000, "Modern apartment with river views, concierge service, private gym."));
42.         repository.save(new Property("Detached house",      "Bristol", "Clifton",       4, 650_000, "Period property with original features, large garden, near Clifton Downs."));
43.         repository.save(new Property("Terraced house",      "Manchester", "Didsbury",   3, 420_000, "Renovated Victorian terrace, open-plan kitchen, good schools nearby."));
44.         repository.save(new Property("Flat",                "Edinburgh", "New Town",    2, 380_000, "Georgian conversion, high ceilings, communal garden, central location."));
45.         repository.save(new Property("Bungalow",            "Brighton", "Hove",         2, 480_000, "Single-storey, fully accessible, large decked garden, quiet street."));
46.         repository.save(new Property("Detached house",      "London", "Wimbledon",      5, 1_200_000, "Spacious family home, double garage, large south-facing garden."));
47.         repository.save(new Property("Flat",                "Leeds", "City Centre",     1, 180_000, "High-spec studio, roof terrace, city views, ideal for professionals."));
48.         repository.save(new Property("Semi-detached house", "Birmingham", "Moseley",    4, 390_000, "Extended family home, two bathrooms, near excellent schools."));
49.         repository.save(new Property("Cottage",             "Oxford", "Headington",     3, 560_000, "Charming stone cottage, private parking, walking distance to JR Hospital."));
50.         LOG.info("Seeded 10 properties.");
51.     }
52. 
53.     /**
54.      * Searches the property database using the given criteria.
55.      * String parameters may be null or empty to skip that filter.
56.      * Numeric parameters use 0 as a sentinel meaning "no filter".
57.      *
58.      * @param type        Property type substring (e.g. "flat", "house"); null or blank = no filter
59.      * @param city        City substring (e.g. "London", "Bristol"); null or blank = no filter
60.      * @param minBedrooms Minimum number of bedrooms; 0 = no minimum
```

```
ID: 3548136463, ReviewID: 4658913402
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/index.xhtml, Line: 48
Body: `p:remoteCommand` defaults `process` to `@form` (PrimeFaces RemoteCommand docs), so every WebSocket-triggered refresh will submit/validate the whole form. With `enquiryInput required="true"` (and it often being empty after a submit), validation can fail and block `pipelineGrid` updates, breaking the real-time pipeline refresh chain.
---
ID: 3548136488, ReviewID: 4658913402
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/index.xhtml, Line: 84
Body: `agent.enquiry` is user-supplied input and is currently rendered via template text (`#{agent.enquiry}`), which can emit unescaped HTML and enable XSS. Render it via a JSF component with escaping (e.g., `h:outputText`).
---
ID: 3548136497, ReviewID: 4658913402
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/index.xhtml, Line: 87
Body: `agent.currentIntent` originates from the model/tool and can contain arbitrary text; rendering it as template text can emit unescaped HTML. Use `h:outputText` (escape=true) to prevent XSS.
---
ID: 3548136511, ReviewID: 4658913402
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/PropertyDatabase.java, Line: 38
Body: `PropertyRepository.findAll()` is documented here as returning a Stream; the stream should be closed to avoid leaking persistence resources. Wrap the `count()` call in try-with-resources.
---
ID: 3548136521, ReviewID: 4658913402
Path: src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/PropertyDatabase.java, Line: 77
Body: Same Stream-lifecycle issue as above: `repository.findAll().toList()` should close the underlying Stream (especially if backed by JPA). Use try-with-resources around the stream before filtering.
```

```
36.     @Transactional
37.     public void doSeedDatabase() {
38.         long count = repository.findAll().count();
39.         if (count > 0) {
40.             LOG.info("Property database already seeded with " + count + " properties.");
41.             return;
42.         }
43.         LOG.info("Seeding property database...");

50.         repository.save(new Property("Detached house",      "London", "Wimbledon",      5, 1_200_000, "Spacious family home, double garage, large south-facing garden."));
51.         repository.save(new Property("Flat",                "Leeds", "City Centre",     1, 180_000, "High-spec studio, roof terrace, city views, ideal for professionals."));
52.         repository.save(new Property("Semi-detached house", "Birmingham", "Moseley",    4, 390_000, "Extended family home, two bathrooms, near excellent schools."));
53.         repository.save(new Property("Cottage",             "Oxford", "Headington",     3, 560_000, "Charming stone cottage, private parking, walking distance to JR Hospital."));
54.         LOG.info("Seeded 10 properties.");
55.     }
56. 
57.     /**
58.      * Searches the property database using the given criteria.
59.      * String parameters may be null or empty to skip that filter.
60.      * Numeric parameters use 0 as a sentinel meaning "no filter".
61.      *
62.      * @param type        Property type substring (e.g. "flat", "house"); null or blank = no filter
63.      * @param city        City substring (e.g. "London", "Bristol"); null or blank = no filter
64.      * @param minBedrooms Minimum number of bedrooms; 0 = no minimum
65.      * @param maxPriceGbp Maximum price in GBP; 0 = no maximum
66.      * @return Matching properties, up to 10 results
67.      */
68.     @CopilotTool(value = "Searches the real estate listings database. Returns up to 10 matching properties.",
69.                  name = "search_properties")
70.     @Transactional
71.     public List<Property> searchProperties(
72.             @CopilotToolParam("Property type substring (e.g. 'flat', 'house', 'bungalow')") String type,
73.             @CopilotToolParam("City substring (e.g. 'London', 'Bristol')") String city,
74.             @CopilotToolParam("Minimum number of bedrooms (0 for no minimum)") int minBedrooms,
75.             @CopilotToolParam("Maximum price in GBP (0 for no maximum)") double maxPriceGbp) {
76. 
77.         List<Property> results = repository.findAll().toList();
78. 
79.         if (type != null && !type.isBlank()) {
80.             String ltype = type.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
81.             results = results.stream()
82.                 .filter(p -> p.getType().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains(ltype))
83.                 .toList();
84.         }
85.         if (city != null && !city.isBlank()) {
86.             String lcity = city.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
87.             results = results.stream()
88.                 .filter(p -> p.getCity().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains(lcity))
89.                 .toList();
90.         }
91.         if (minBedrooms > 0) {
92.             results = results.stream()
93.                 .filter(p -> p.getBedrooms() >= minBedrooms)
94.                 .toList();
95.         }
96.         if (maxPriceGbp > 0) {
97.             results = results.stream()
98.                 .filter(p -> p.getPriceGbp() <= maxPriceGbp)
99.                 .toList();
100.         }
```

```
* Represents a single real-estate enquiry agent session.\n+ * Each agent owns a CopilotSession that runs on a virtual 
thread.\n+ *\n+ * <p>Demonstrates three Copilot SDK tool definition styles:\n+ * <ol>\n+ *   <li>{@code @CopilotTool} 
annotation — {@code setCurrentPhase}</li>\n+ *   <li>{@code ToolDefinition.from(...)} lambda — {@code

startedAt = Instant.now();\n+    private volatile Instant finishedAt;\n+    private CopilotSession session;\n+\n+    
public Agent(String id, String enquiry, PropertyDatabase propertyDatabase,\n+                 UiUpdateSocket 
uiUpdateSocket) {\n+        this.id = id;\n+        this.enquiry = enquiry;\n+        this.propertyDatabase = 
propertyDatabase;\n+        this.uiUpdateSocket = uiUpdateSocket;\n+    }\n+\n+    /**\n+     * Runs the agent session 
against the given CopilotClient.\n+     * Blocks (on a virtual thread) until the session completes.\n+     */\n+    
public void run(CopilotClient client) {\n+        SystemMessageConfig systemMessage = new SystemMessageConfig()\n+     
           .setMode(SystemMessageMode.CUSTOMIZE);\n+        
systemMessage.getSections().put(SystemMessageSection.IDENTITY,\n+                new SectionOverride()\n+              
          .setAction(SectionOverrideAction.REPLACE)\n+                        .setContent(\"\"\"\n+                    
        You are part of a real estate recommendation system. You will receive enquiries\n+                            
from customers, and you must carry out the following workflow. As you proceed,\n+                            update 
your current phase and intent, which will be visible to the user.\n+                            Do not stop until the 
phase reaches a final state.\n+                            Start by setting phase to \"VALIDATING\".\n+\n+

stop.\n+                            - Search phase\n+                              - Extract relevant search criteria 
and search our property listings.\n+                              - To search our property listings, call the 
search_properties tool.\n+                                You may call it multiple times with different filters to 
refine results.\n+                              - At the end of this phase, if you don't find any relevant 
properties,\n+                                set phase to \"REJECTED_NO_MATCHES\" and stop.\n+

customer.\n+                              - Your report should include a summary of the customer's needs and the 
top\n+                                1-3 matching properties. For each property, include key selling points.\n+       
                       - At the end of this phase, set phase to \"DONE\" and stop.\n+\n+
```

```
1. package com.microsoft.build.realestate.data;
2. 
3. import com.microsoft.build.realestate.Property;
4. import jakarta.data.repository.BasicRepository;
5. import jakarta.data.repository.By;
6. import jakarta.data.repository.Find;
7. import jakarta.data.repository.Query;
8. import jakarta.data.repository.Repository;
9. import java.util.List;
10. 
11. /**
12.  * Jakarta Data repository for Property entities.
13.  * Extends BasicRepository to inherit save() and findAll() (as Stream).
14.  * Uses @By annotations for explicit parameter binding (no -parameters compiler flag needed).
15.  */
16. @Repository
17. public interface PropertyRepository extends BasicRepository<Property, Long> {
18. 
19.     @Find
20.     List<Property> findByType(@By("type") String type);
21. 
22.     @Find
23.     List<Property> findByCity(@By("city") String city);
24. 
25.     @Query("WHERE bedrooms >= ?1")
26.     List<Property> findByBedroomsAtLeast(int minBedrooms);
27. 
28.     @Query("WHERE priceGbp <= ?1")
29.     List<Property> findByPriceAtMost(double maxPrice);
30. }
```
